###Intro###
country_event = {
	id = tram.intro
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.intro"
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = TRM_visit_from_japan
			activate_mission = TRM_oblastniki_committee
			activate_mission = TRM_nra_sabotage
			activate_mission = TRM_lessons_of_kolchak_putsch
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 505058 }
				unit_leader_event = { id = tram.2 days = 646 random_days = 100 }
				unit_leader_event = { id = tram.3 days = 646 random_days = 100 }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = tram_crisis_1936.1
				days = 85
				random_days = 35
			}
			country_event = {
				id = tram_crisis_1936.3
				days = 130
				random_days = 35
			}
			country_event = {
				id = tram_crisis_1936.4
				days = 170
				random_days = 35
			}
			RUS = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1937.1
					days = 285
					random_days = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
	title = tram.intro.t
	desc = tram.intro.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.intro.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = trammlad.147
				days = 10
			}
			country_event = {
				id = tram.993
				days = 20
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.intro.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		country_event = tram.999
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = trammlad.147
				days = 10
			}
			country_event = {
				id = tram.993
				days = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = tram.994001
	immediate = {
		annex_country = { target = SIB transfer_troops = yes }
	}
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Ivan Lavrov"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		SIB = {
			exists = yes
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Ivan Lavrov"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 } 
	fire_only_once = yes
}

country_event = {
	id = tram.994002
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		has_global_flag = RCW_begun
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RCW_over }
		RUS = { exists = no }
		RRF = { exists = no }
		WRA = { exists = no }
		RVA = { exists = no }
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.994002.a
		RUS = { clr_country_flag = soviet_speaking_tag }
		set_global_flag = RCW_over
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_rrf_state = yes
					state = 821
					state = 880
					state = 209
					state = 210
					state = 1287
					state = 1290
					state = 1289
					state = 1288
					state = 1291
				}
			}
			add_core_of = RUS
			remove_core_of = RRF
			remove_core_of = WRA
		}
	}
}

###Transamur breaks away###

country_event = { #Transamur breaks away!
	id = tram.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.1" }
	title = tram.1.t
	desc = tram.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #war
		name = tram.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_japan_intervention option = TRM_JAPAN_INTERVENTION_FALSE }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = PRI_breaksaway
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = {
				TRM_remove_japanese_influence = yes
			}
		JAP = {
			remove_from_faction = TRM
			if = {
				limit = { has_war_with = RUS }
				RUS = { save_event_target_as = white_peace_receiver }
				white_peace_with_TARGET = yes
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = TRM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	}
	option = { #leave them
		name = tram.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_japan_intervention option = TRM_JAPAN_INTERVENTION_TRUE }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = PRI_breaksaway
		add_stability = -0.15
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = {
				TRM_remove_japanese_influence = yes
				set_temp_variable = { target = JAP }
				clear_all_relations_with_TARGET = yes
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			remove_from_faction = TRM
		}
	}
}
unit_leader_event = { #Diterikhs dies
	id = tram.2
	immediate = { set_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead }
	title = tram.2.t
	desc = tram.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		ROOT = { TRM_do_rovs_in_power = yes }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = tram.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}	
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_unit_leader = 505058
				}
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 505058 }			
					remove_unit_leader = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						ruling_only = yes
						name = "Mikhail Diterikhs"
					}
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Vladimir Kappel"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Vladimir_Kappel.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = junta_subtype
				}
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 505060 }
				promote_leader = yes
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = TRM_Vladimir_Kappel_hog_pau  
		}
	}	
}
unit_leader_event = { #Diterikhs dies
	id = tram.3
	immediate = { set_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead }
	title = tram.2.t
	desc = tram.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		ROOT = { 
			TRM_do_rovs_in_power = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead }
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.3.a
		ROOT = {
			add_political_power = 25
			add_stability = -0.01
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_unit_leader = 505058
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 505058 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 505060 }
				promote_leader = yes
			}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Vladimir Kappel"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Vladimir_Kappel.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = junta_subtype
			}
		}		
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Kirill dies
	id = tram.5
	title = {
		text = rusd.95.t.tsar

			NOT = { has_government = national_populist }
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = trammlad.505.t

			has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Kirill I" }

	}

	}

			name = "Vladimir III"
			desc = "POLITICS_VLADIMIR_ROMANOV_ABS_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Vladimir_Romanov.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = absolute_monarchy_subtype
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rusd.95.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Kirill I"
			}
			OR = {
				TRM_Mlad_in_power = yes
				has_government = national_populist 
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = Kirill_Romanov_dead
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Vladimir III"
			desc = "POLITICS_VLADIMIR_ROMANOV_CON_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Vladimir_III.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"

				name = "Vladimir III"
				desc = "POLITICS_VLADIMIR_ROMANOV_CON_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Vladimir_III.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"

			}
		}
		set_country_flag = TRM_TSAR_VLAD
		set_country_flag = Kirill_Romanov_dead

		name = rusd.95.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {

					ruling_only = yes
					name = "Kirill I"
				} 
			}
		}	
		set_country_flag = Kirill_Romanov_dead
		add_political_power = -15
	}
}

		add_stability = 0.1

			country_event = {
				id = tram.22
				days = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.13
				days = 75
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = tram.24
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.24" }
	title = tram.24.t
	desc = tram.24.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.24.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = RUS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = russianews.7
				days = 1
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = RUS }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = russianews.7
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.24.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		RUS = {
			transfer_state = 565
			transfer_state = 563
			transfer_state = 564
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				has_country_flag = TRM_oblastniki_operate
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.15
			}
		}
	}

###Soviets transfer states###
country_event = {
	id = tram.25
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.25" }
	title = tram.25.t
	desc = tram.25.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.25.a
		TRM = {
			transfer_state = 566
			566 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			transfer_state = 644
			644 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			transfer_state = 1202
			1202 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = TRM_control_FE
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = JAP
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram.42
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = tram.48
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.48" }
	title = tram.48.t
	desc = tram.48.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { #Submit
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
			factor = 1000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI
				}
			}
		}
		name = tram.48.a
		JAP = {
			country_event = tram.49
		}
	}
	option = { #Break away
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
		}
		name = tram.48.b
		set_global_flag = TRM_relations_JAP_broke
		embargo_FROM = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.2
		}

			limit = {
				TRM = { is_subject_of = JAP }
			}
			JAP = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = TRM
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.150
				days = 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = {
				TRM_remove_japanese_influence = yes
				set_temp_variable = { target = JAP }
				clear_all_relations_with_TARGET = yes
			}
			JAP = {			
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = TRM
					relation = docking_rights
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Replace HOS - JAP event
	id = tram.49
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.49" }
	title = tram.49.t
	desc = tram.49.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { #Mitsue
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
			factor = 1000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				TRM = {
					TRM_japanese_in_power = yes
				}
			}
		}
		name = tram.49.a
		JAP = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = TRM
				autonomy_state = kr_occupied_puppet
			}
		}
		TRM = {
			remove_country_leader_trait = TRM_shaky_rule
			remove_ideas = TRM_dream
			hidden_effect = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					popularity = 40
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					TRM_Grigoriy_M_Semyenov_hog_pau
					BRT_Ivan_P_Kalmykov_for_pau
					BRT_Leonid_V_Verigo_eco_pau
					TRM_Boris_Shepunov_sec_pau
				}
			}			
			if = {
				limit = { 
					country_exists = TRB
					TRB = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {

								has_id = 243912
							}
						}
						set_nationality = TRM
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						TRB = { is_ai = no }
					}
					TRM = { change_tag_from = TRB }
				}
			}
			country_event = tram.50
		}
	}

				}
			}

country_event = {
	id = tram.80
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.80"
		#game rule ai cheat
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_KOLCHAK_SECURES_POWER
				}
				is_ai = yes
				check_variable = { TRM_Overall_Kolchak_Support < 0.3 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { TRM_Overall_Kolchak_Support = 0.1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MONARCHY
				}
				is_ai = yes
				check_variable = { ROVSOrientation > -0 }
			}
			set_variable = { ROVSOrientation = -1 }
		}
	}
	title = tram.80.t
	desc = tram.80.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Kolchak survived
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NEW_MILITARY_CABINET
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MORYAKI_IN_POWER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_OBLASTNIKI
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV
					}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = tramnews.2
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Kolchak survived with Japanese help
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path

					}

					}

					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_KOLCHAK_SECURES_POWER
				}
			}

						}

							rule = TRM_path 
							option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_OBLASTNIKI
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = TRM_path 
							option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = TRM_path 
							option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = TRM_path 
							option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MLADOROSSI
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = TRM_path 
							option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NATSI
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = tram.80.c

				desc = "POLITICS_MIKHAIL_DITERIKHS"

				traits = {}
			}
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			long_name = TRM_rovs_party_long
			name = TRM_rovs_party
		}

			}
		}
	}

				name = TRM_semyonov_party
			}

				set_political_party = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = 41
			}

						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						country_exists = TRB
						TRB = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							TRB = { has_idea = UCH_union_of_cossack_hosts }
						}

					}

							limit = {
								OR = {
									has_id = 243910

									has_id = 505056

									has_id = 243912
								}
							}
							set_nationality = ROOT
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							TRB = { is_ai = no }
						}
						ROOT = { change_tag_from = TRB }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Oi Shigemoto
		name = tram.91.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
	}

###Japanese delegation trying to owerthrow you###
country_event = {
	id = tram.119
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.119" }
	title = tram.119.t
	desc = tram.119.d

	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		check_variable = { party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat > 0.34 }
		TRM_has_japanese_influence = yes
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				TRM_japanese_in_power = yes
				has_idea = TRM_Grigoriy_M_Semyenov_hog_pau
				TRM_semyenov_in_power = yes
				has_war = yes
			}
			has_country_flag = TRM_delegation_bypass
		}
	}

		months = 1
	}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}

				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat

			}
		}

		restore_previous_government_type = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {

							}
						}

					}

					limit = {

					}

				}
			}

			factor = 1000
		}

			OR = {
				has_game_rule = {

				}

				}

				}

				}

				}

					set_country_flag = TRM_agitation

					set_country_flag = TRM_bad_agitation
				}

			}
		}

		TRM = { embargo_PREV = yes }

	desc = tram.1005.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		NOT = { country_exists = TRM }
		NOT = { 408 = { is_owned_by = JAP } }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	option = {
		name = tram.1005.a
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = {
				TRM_remove_japanese_influence = yes
				set_temp_variable = { target = JAP }
				clear_all_relations_with_TARGET = yes
			}
			JAP = {			
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = TRM
					relation = docking_rights
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

			}

		}

		add_popularity = {

				is_ai = yes
			}
		}

				disband = yes

				disband = yes
			}
		}

				target = TRM
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.154.b

			TRM = {

			}

country_event = { #russian empire in exile
	id = tram.155
	title = tram.155.t
	desc = tram.155.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = tram.154.b
		retire_country_leader = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_TSAR
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Kirill_Romanov_dead } }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Kirill I"
				desc = "POLITICS_KIRILL_ROMANOV_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Kyril_Romanov.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = absolute_monarchy_subtype
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Vladimir III"
				desc = "POLITICS_VLADIMIR_ROMANOV_ABS_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Vladimir_Romanov.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = absolute_monarchy_subtype
			}
		}
		add_ideas = one_and_indivisible
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = { set_country_flag = Kirill_Romanov_dead }
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_completed_focus = RUS_Orthodox_Eurasianists
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					country_event = {
						id = tram.1590
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				RUS = {
					country_event = {
						id = tram.159
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = tram.158
				days = 2
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rusd.204
				days = 60
				random_days = 344
			}
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = tramnews.3
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 565
					state = 564

				}
			}
			transfer_state_to = TRB
			add_core_of = TRB
			remove_core_of = TRM
			add_claim_by = TRM
		}
		TRB = { 
			transfer_technology_without_doctrines = yes
			division_template = {
				name = "Kazatskaya Diviziya"
				division_names_group = TRM_CAV_01
				regiments = {
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 563 }
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Kazatskaya Diviziya\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
					owner = TRB

country_event = { #TRM wants to join us
	id = trmnra.14
	title = trmnra.14.t
	desc = trmnra.14.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = trmnra.14.a
		add_stability = 0.025
		TRM = {
			every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			every_owned_state = { 
				limit = { is_core_of = PREV }
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
					remove_claim_by = ROOT
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		TRM = {
			disband_one_to_three_divisions = yes
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Kazatskaya Diviziya"
				disband = yes
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Veteranskaya Diviziya"
				disband = yes
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Chekhoslovatskiy Korpus"
				disband = yes
			}
		}
		annex_country = { target = TRM transfer_troops = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { TRM = { is_ai = no } }
			ROOT = { 
				change_tag_from = TRM
			}
		}		
	}
}

country_event = { #last bastion of bolshevism
	id = trmnra.16
	title = trmnra.16.t
	desc = trmnra.16.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = trmnra.16.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
			factor = 1000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP_RADSOC
				}
			}
			modifier = {
			factor = 1000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP
				}
			}
		}
		retire_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Alexander Krasnoshchyokov"
			desc = "POLITICS_KRASNOSHSCHYOKOV_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Alexander_Krasnoshchyokov.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = authcom_subtype
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
		}
		set_temp_variable = { nra_popularity = party_popularity_100@totalist }
		set_political_party = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = var:nra_popularity
		}
		remove_ideas = TRM_dream
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_core_of = RUS
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		set_temp_variable = { change_morale = -0.15 }
		RUS_change_siberian_war_morale = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_SOV
	}
	option = {
		name = trmnra.16.a2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
			factor = 1000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP_RADSOC
				}
			}
			modifier = {
			factor = 1000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP
				}
			}
		}
		retire_country_leader = yes		
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Pyetr Nikiforov"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Pyetr_Nikiforov.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = authcom_subtype
		}
		remove_ideas = TRM_dream
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_core_of = RUS
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		set_temp_variable = { change_morale = -0.15 }
		RUS_change_siberian_war_morale = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_SOV
	}
	option = {
		name = trmnra.16.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP_BOLSHEVIKS }
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP_FRUNZE }
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP_TUKHA }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = {
					has_socialist_government = no
					NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
				}
			}
			RUS = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_trait = hidden_sympathies
					}
					remove_unit_leader_trait = hidden_sympathies
					set_nationality = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_unit_leader = 1955
						has_unit_leader = 1954
						RUS = { 
							NOT = { has_country_flag = Grigory_Zinoviev_dead }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = trmnra.100
				days = 7
			}		
		}
		add_stability = 0.1		
		set_country_flag = SOV_restored_in_transamur
		unlock_decision_tooltip = RUS_Start_The_Offensive_TRM
	}
	option = {
		name = trmnra.16.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = trmnra.102
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event trmnra.102" }

	is_triggered_only = yes

country_event = {
	id = trmnra.103
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event trmnra.103" }
	title = trmnra.103.t
	desc = trmnra.103.d
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		TRM_nra_in_power = yes
		has_idea = TRM_dream
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = trmnra.103.a
		remove_ideas = TRM_dream
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = RCW_joint_front_idea }
			remove_ideas = RCW_joint_front_idea
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_core_of = RUS
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		set_temp_variable = { change_morale = -0.15 }
		RUS_change_siberian_war_morale = yes
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
			}
			country_event = trmnra.104
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			every_enemy_country = {
				ROOT = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_SOV
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 1955 }
			set_nationality = ROOT
			unit_leader_event = {
				id = russia.1925
				days = 1
				random = 24
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader_flag = SOV_british_clique }
			set_nationality = ROOT
		}
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 1956 }
			set_nationality = ROOT
			unit_leader_event = {
				id = russia.1926
				days = 1
				random = 24
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader_flag = SOV_french_clique }
			set_nationality = ROOT
		}
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 1954 }
			set_nationality = ROOT
			unit_leader_event = {
				id = russia.1924
				days = 1
				random = 24
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader_flag = SOV_italian_clique }
			set_nationality = ROOT
		}
	}

	option = { #
		name = trmnra.103.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		FROM = {
			country_event = trmnra.105
		}		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FROM
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 1 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 2 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_political_power = -30
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 3 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.15
			add_political_power = -60
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = TRM }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = russianews.7
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
	
	trigger = {

		TRM_nra_in_power = yes
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = trmnra.106.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_siberia = yes
					is_central_asia = yes
				}
				NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
				is_owned_by = FROM
			}
			transfer_state_to = ROOT
			if = {
				limit = { is_siberia = yes }
				remove_core_of = FROM
				add_claim_by = FROM
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_owned_by = ROOT
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
						}
						ROOT = { divisions_in_state = { state = PREV size > 0 } }
					}
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = { tag = ROOT }
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = ROOT
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
						}
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
				}
			}
			remove_puppet_and_leave_faction = yes
		}		
		add_ideas = TRM_dream
		FROM = {
			country_event = trmnra.105
		}		
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = TRM_SOV }
			set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_NRA

				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 1 }

			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -15
		}

				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 2 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_political_power = -30
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 3 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.15
			add_political_power = -60
		}

				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = TRM }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = russianews.7
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #
		name = trmnra.106.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		}
		remove_ideas = TRM_dream
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_core_of = RUS
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}

			set_nationality = ROOT
			unit_leader_event = {
				id = russia.1925
				days = 1
				random = 24
			}
		}

			limit = { has_unit_leader_flag = SOV_british_clique }
			set_nationality = ROOT
		}

			set_nationality = ROOT

		hidden_effect = { 
			complete_national_focus = TRM_Nationalists_Take_Over

			}
		}
	}

						ruling_only = yes

				}

			NOT = { has_country_flag = Kirill_Romanov_dead }
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Kirill I"
			desc = "POLITICS_KYRIL_ROMANOV_MLAD_DESC"

							name = "Kirill I"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}

					}

		}

			RUS = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Kirill I"
						ruling_only = yes
					}

						name = "Vladimir III"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}

	id = tram.309
	title = tram.309.t
	desc = tram.309.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = tram.309.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.2
			}
			add_stability = 0.3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.3
				has_stability > 0.2
			}
			add_stability = 0.25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.4
				has_stability > 0.3
			}
			add_stability = 0.2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.5
				has_stability > 0.4
			}
			add_stability = 0.15
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_support < 0.5
			}
			add_war_support = 0.15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.6
				has_stability > 0.5
			}
			add_stability = 0.1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.7
				has_stability > 0.6
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability > 0.7
				has_stability < 1
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_20 = yes
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_siberia = yes
				NOT = { is_core_of = TRM }
				OR = {
					is_core_of = SOV
					is_core_of = RUS
				}
			}
			TRM = { add_state_core = PREV }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = tram_crisis_1937.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram_crisis_1937.5" }
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = RUS }
					NOT = { tag = TRM }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1937.16
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	title = tram_crisis_1937.5.t
	desc = tram_crisis_1937.5.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	option = {
		name = tram_crisis_1937.5.a
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = prepare_for_war
			id = FROM
			value = -1000
		}
		FROM = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = prepare_for_war
				id = FROM
				value = -1000
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = TRM_anti_air_defences
					has_country_flag = TRM_border_control
				}
				country_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1937.6
					days = 5
					random_days = 7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					count_triggers = {
						amount = 1
						has_country_flag = TRM_anti_air_defences
						has_country_flag = TRM_border_control
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1937.8
					days = 5
					random_days = 7
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1937.7
					days = 5
					random_days = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram_crisis_1937.5.b
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				RUS_dont_attack_if_vulnerable_or_preparing = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_target_is_stronger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_faction_is_stronger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_overlord_is_stronger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					russian_civil_war = yes
					FROM = { tag = RUS }
					TRM_nra_game_rule = yes
				}
			}
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = prepare_for_war
			id = FROM
			value = -1000
		}
		FROM = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = prepare_for_war
				id = FROM
				value = -1000
			}
		}
		activate_decision = RUS_Start_The_Offensive_TRM
	}
}
